|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1871">**Fonctionnalité**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1871">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1872">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1872">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1873">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1873">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1874">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1874">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1875">Taille maximale de la boîte aux lettres d'arbitrage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1875">Maximum size of the arbitration mailbox</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1876">10 Go</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1876">10 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1877">10 Go</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1877">10 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1878">10 Go</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1878">10 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1879">Nombre maximal de modérateurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1879">Maximum number of moderators</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1880">10 modérateurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1880">10 moderators</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1881">10 modérateurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1881">10 moderators</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1882">10 modérateurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1882">10 moderators</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1883">Expiration des messages en attente de modération</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1883">Expiration for messages waiting for moderation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1884">2 jours</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1884">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1885">2 jours</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1885">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1886">2 jours</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1886">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1887">Débit maximal de messages de notification d'expiration du délai de modération</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1887">Maximum rate for expired moderation notification messages</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1888">300 notifications d'expiration par heure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1888">300 expiration notifications per hour</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1889">300 notifications d'expiration par heure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1889">300 expiration notifications per hour</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1890">300 notifications d'expiration par heure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1890">300 expiration notifications per hour</span></span>  <br/> |
   
#### <a name="exchange-activesync-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1891">Limites d'ActiveSync Exchange</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1891">Exchange ActiveSync limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1892"><a name="bkmk_ExchangeActiveSync_Limits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1892"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1893">Les limites suivantes s'appliquent à Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync, un protocole client qui synchronise les données de boîtes aux lettres entre les appareils mobiles et Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1893">The following limits apply to Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync, a client protocol that synchronizes mailbox data between mobile devices and Exchange.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1894">Limite de l'appareil **Exchange ActiveSync** Le nombre maximal d'appareils Exchange ActiveSync par boîte aux lettres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1894">**Exchange ActiveSync device limit** The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices per mailbox.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1895">Limite de suppression de l'appareil **Exchange ActiveSync** Le nombre maximal d'appareils Exchange ActiveSync qu'un administrateur Exchange peut supprimer en un mois.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1895">**Exchange ActiveSync device deletion limit** The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices that an Exchange administrator can delete in a single month.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1896">**Limite des pièces jointes Exchange ActiveSync** La taille maximale d'une pièce jointe de message qui peut être envoyée ou reçue par un appareil Exchange ActiveSync.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1896">**Exchange ActiveSync file attachment limit** The maximum size of a message file attachment that can be sent or received by an Exchange ActiveSync device.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1897">**Fonctionnalité**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1897">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1898">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1898">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1899">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1899">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1900">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1900">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1901">Limite de l'appareil Exchange ActiveSync</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1901">Exchange ActiveSync device limit</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1902">100</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1902">100</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1903">100</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1903">100</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1904">100</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1904">100</span></span>  <br/> |

## <a name="onedrive-for-business-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1913">Fonctionnalités de OneDrive Entreprise</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1913">OneDrive for Business features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1914"><a name="OfcOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1914"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1915">OneDrive entreprise (anciennement SkyDrive Pro) est un espace de stockage en ligne personnel dans le Cloud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1915">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage space in the cloud.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1916">Utilisez-le pour stocker vos fichiers professionnels sur plusieurs appareils avec facilité et sécurité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1916">Use it to store your work files across multiple devices with ease and security.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1917">Partagez vos fichiers avec des collègues en fonction de vos besoins, et modifiez les documents Office en temps réel avec Office Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1917">Share your files with colleagues as needed, and edit Office documents together in real time with Office Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1918">Synchronisez les fichiers sur votre ordinateur local à l'aide de l'application de synchronisation OneDrive entreprise.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1918">Sync files to your local computer using the OneDrive for Business sync app.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1919">OneDrive Entreprise est inclus dans SharePoint Online et peut également être acheté sous forme de plan autonome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1919">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1920">L'option OneDrive Entreprise autonome inclut Office Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1920">The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1921">Pour en savoir plus, consultez la rubrique [qu'est-ce que OneDrive entreprise?](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=271073)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1921">To learn more, see [What is OneDrive for Business?](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=271073)</span></span>

### <a name="onedrive-for-business-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1925">Limites de OneDrive entreprise</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1925">OneDrive for Business limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1926">OneDrive entreprise plan 1 fournit 1 to d'espace de stockage par utilisateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1926">OneDrive for Business Plan 1 provides 1 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1927">Les offres de qualification suivantes fournissent un espace de stockage OneDrive illimité par utilisateur pour les abonnements avec au moins cinq utilisateurs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1927">The following qualifying plans provide unlimited OneDrive storage per user for subscriptions with at least five users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1928">Microsoft fournira 5 to d'espace de stockage initial par utilisateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1928">Microsoft will provide an initial 5 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1929">Les clients qui souhaitent disposer d'un espace de stockage OneDrive supplémentaire peuvent le demander si nécessaire en contactant le support Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1929">Customers who want additional OneDrive storage can request it as needed by contacting Microsoft Support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1930">Les abonnements avec moins de cinq utilisateurs reçoivent 1 to de stockage par utilisateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1930">Subscriptions with less than five users receive 1 TB of storage per user.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1931">Office 365 A1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1931">Office 365 A1</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1932">Office 365 A3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1932">Office 365 A3</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1933">Office 365 A5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1933">Office 365 A5</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1934">Vous ne pouvez pas allouer davantage de stockage à un utilisateur OneDrive spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1934">You cannot allocate more storage to a specific OneDrive user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1935">Toutefois, vous pouvez réduire la quantité de stockage qu'un utilisateur voit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1935">However, you can lower the amount of storage that a user sees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1936">Si un utilisateur d'Office 365 Enterprise F1 a besoin de plus de stockage, vous devez effectuer une mise à niveau vers Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1936">If an Office 365 Enterprise F1 user needs more storage, then you'll need to upgrade to Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1937">Pour plus d'informations sur les types de fichiers que vous ne pouvez pas ajouter à OneDrive entreprise, consultez [la rubrique types de fichiers qui ne peuvent pas être ajoutés à une liste ou une bibliothèque](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=273757).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1937">For information about file types that you can't add to OneDrive for Business, see [Types of files that cannot be added to a list or library](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=273757).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1938">OneDrive Entreprise est inclus dans SharePoint Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1938">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-1939">Pour en savoir plus sur les limitations supplémentaires dans SharePoint Online, telles que les quotas de collection de sites, les limites de chargement de fichiers et les limites de stockage, voir limites [et frontières logicielles pour SharePoint Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=271273).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-1939">To learn about additional limitations in SharePoint Online, such as site collection quotas, file upload limits, and storage limits, see [SharePoint Online software boundaries and limits](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=271273).</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3471">Limites de Skype entreprise Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3471">Skype for Business Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3472">Les limites de Skype entreprise Online appartiennent aux catégories suivantes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3472">The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3473">Limites pair à pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3473">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#peer-to-peer-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3474">Limites de réunion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3474">Meeting limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3475">Limites de rétention de réunion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3475">Meeting retention limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-retention-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3476">Limites en minutes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3476">Minute limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#minute-limits)
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-p175">Les limites appliquées à une organisation Office 365 peuvent varier selon l'ancienneté de son abonnement au service. En cas de modification d'une limite dans les centres de données Microsoft, l'application de la modification à tous les clients existants peut prendre un certain temps.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-p175">The limits applied to an Office 365 organization can differ depending on how long the organization has been enrolled in the service. When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3479">Limites pair à pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3479">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-p176">**Limite de transfert de fichiers** Taille maximale d'un fichier qui peut être transféré lors d'une conversation par messagerie instantanée dans Skype Entreprise Online. Pour connaître les types de fichiers dont le transfert est bloqué, consultez l'article du support Microsoft sur [l'envoi ou la réception de fichiers ou de pièces jointes dans Skype Entreprise Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=398280).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-p176">**File transfer limit** The maximum size of a file that can be transferred in a Skype for Business Online IM conversation. To learn which file types are blocked for file transfer, see the Microsoft Support article about [sending and receiving files or attachments in Skype for Business Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=398280).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3482">**Limite des conversations ouvertes dans des onglets** Nombre maximal d'onglets de conversation qu'un utilisateur Skype Entreprise peut ouvrir en même temps.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3482">**Open tabbed conversations limit** The maximum number of conversation tabs that a Skype for Business user can have open at one time.</span></span>

The full participant list remains visible to the presenters in the meeting. Also, Gallery View and IM errors are hidden from the attendees.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="meeting-retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3537">Limites de rétention de réunion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3537">Meeting retention limits</span></span>

#### <a name="minute-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3569">Limites en minutes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3569">Minute limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ccfc4-3570">Pour plus d'informations sur les limitations de minute dans Skype entreprise Online, consultez la rubrique [conditions d'utilisation des services RTC de Skype entreprise Online](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Skype-for-Business-Online-PSTN-services-use-terms-dc6e95cd-51e8-49ca-bcd3-78dc9dae486a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccfc4-3570">For information about minute limitations in Skype for Business Online Domestic and International Calling Plans, see [Skype for Business Online PSTN services use terms](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Skype-for-Business-Online-PSTN-services-use-terms-dc6e95cd-51e8-49ca-bcd3-78dc9dae486a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span>
